        <body>
            <div n="1" type="sthāna">
                <head xml:lang="en">[Sūtrasthāna 32-end]</head>
                <div n="32" type="adhyāya">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.32.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ svabhāvavipratipattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.2">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.32.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.3-4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.32.3-4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svabhāvasiddhānāṃ śarīraikadeśānām anyabhāvitvaṃ maraṇāya | tad yathā-
                        śuklānāṃ kṛṣṇatvaṃ, kṛṣṇānāṃ śuklatā, raktānām anyavarṇatvaṃ, sthirāṇāṃ
                        mṛdutvaṃ , mṛdūnāṃ sthiratā, calānāmacalatvaṃ, acalānāṃ calatā, pṛthūnāṃ
                        saṅkṣiptatvaṃ, saṅkṣiptānāṃ pṛthutā, dīrghāṇāṃ hrasvatvaṃ, hrasvānāṃ
                        dīrghatā, apatanadharmiṇāṃ patanadharmitvaṃ ,
                        patanadharmiṇāmapatanadharmitvamakasmāt, śaity
                        auṣṇyasnaigdhyaraukṣyaprastambhavaivarṇyāvasādanaṃ cāṅgānām ||3|| svebhyaḥ
                        sthānebhyaḥ
                        śarīraikadeśānāmavastrastotkṣiptabhrāntāvakṣiptapatitavimuktanirgatāntargatagurulaghutvāni,
                        pravālavarṇavyaṅgaprādurbhāvo vā'pyakasmāt, sirāṇāṃ ca darśanaṃ lalāṭe,
                        nāsāvaṃśe vā piḍakotpattiḥ , lalāṭe vā prabhātakāle svedaḥ, netrarogādvinā
                        vā'śrupravṛttiḥ, gomayacūrṇaprakāśasya vā rajaso darśanamuttamāṅge nilayanaṃ
                        vā kapotakaṅkakākaprabhṛtīnāṃ, mūtrapurīṣavṛddhirabhuñjānānāṃ, tatpraṇāśo vā
                        bhuñjānānāṃ, stanamūlahṛdayor aḥsu ca śūlotpattayaḥ, madhye śūnatvamanteṣu
                        parimlāyitvaṃ viparyayo vā, tathā'rdhāṅge śvayathuḥ śoṣo 'ṅgapakṣayor vā,
                        naṣṭahīnavikalavikṛtasvaratā vā, vivarṇapuṣpaprādurbhāvo vā
                        dantamukhanakhaśarīreṣu, yasya vā'psu kaphapurīṣaretāṃsi nimajjanti, yasya
                        vā dṛṣṭimaṇḍale bhinnavikṛtāni rūpāṇyālokyante, snehābhyaktakeśāṅga iva yo
                        bhāti, yaś ca durbalo bhaktadveṣātisārābhyāṃ pīḍyate, kāsamānaśca
                        tṛṣṇābhibhūtaḥ, kṣīṇaśchardibhaktadveṣayuktaḥ saphenapūyarudhirodvāmī
                        hatasvaraḥ śūlābhipannaś ca manuṣyaḥ, śūnakaracaraṇavadanaḥkṣīṇo 'nnadveṣī
                        srastapiṇḍikāṃsapāṇipādo jvarakāsābhibhūtaḥ, yas tu pūrvāhṇe bhuktamaparāhṇe
                        chardayatyavidagdhamatisāryate vā sa śvāsānmriyate, bastavadvilapan yaśca
                        bhūmau patati srastamuṣkaḥ, stabdhameḍhro bhagnagrīvaḥ pranaṣṭamehanaśca
                        manuṣyaḥ, prāgviśuṣyamāṇāhṛdaya ārdraśarīraḥ, yaś ca loṣṭaṃ loṣṭenābhihanti
                        kāṣṭhaṃ kāṣṭhena, tṛṇāni vā chinatti, adharoṣṭhaṃ daśati, uttaroṣṭhaṃ vā
                        leḍhi, āluñcati vā karṇau keśāṃśca; devadvijagurusuhṛdvaidyāṃś ca dveṣṭi,
                        yasya vakrānuvakragā grahā garhitasthānagatāḥ pīḍayanti, janmarkṣaṃ vā,
                        yasyolkāśanibhyāmabhihanyate horā vā,
                        gṛhadāraśayanāsanayānavāhanamaṇiratnopakaraṇagarhitalakṣaṇanimittaprādurbhāvo
                        veti ||4|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.32.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra
                        <caesura/>
                         cikitsyamānaḥ samyak ca vikāro yo 'bhivardhate |
                        <caesura/>
                         prakṣīṇabalamāṃsasya lakṣaṇaṃ tadgatāyuṣaḥ ||5|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.32.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nivartate mahāvyādhiḥ sahasā yasya dehinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         na cāhāraphalaṃ yasya dṛśyate sa vinaśyati ||6||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.32.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         etāny ariṣṭarūpāṇi samyag budhyeta yo bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhyāsādhyaparīkṣāyāṃ sa rājñaḥ sammato bhavet ||7|| </l>

                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne svabhāvavipratipattirnāma
                        dvātriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||32||</p>
                </div>


                <div n="33" type="adhyāya">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto 'vāraṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.2">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         upadravais tu ye juṣṭā vyādhayo yānty avāryatām |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasāyanād vinā vatsa! tān śṛṇv ekamanā mama ||3|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātavyādhiḥ pramehaś ca kuṣṭham arśo bhagandaram |
                        <caesura/>
                         aśmarī mūḍhagarbhaś ca tathaivodaram aṣṭamam ||4|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aṣṭāv ete prakṛtyaiva duścikitsyā mahāgadāḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         prāṇamāṃsakṣayaḥ śoṣastṛṣṇā cchardirjvaras tathā ||5||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atīsāraś ca mūrcchā ca hikkā śvāsas tathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         etair upadravair juṣṭān sarvāneva vivarjayet ||6|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śūnaṃ suptatvacaṃ bhagnaṃ kampādhmānanipīḍitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         naraṃ rujārtamantaś ca vātavyādhir vināśayet ||7|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathoktopadravāviṣṭam atiprasrutam eva vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         piḍakāpīḍitaṃ gāḍhaṃ prameho hanti mānavam ||8|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prabhinna prasrutāṅgaṃ ca raktanetraṃ hatasvaram |
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcakarmaguṇātītaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ hantīha kuṣṭhinam ||9|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tṛṣṇārocakaśūlārtam atiprasrutaśoṇitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śophātīsārasaṃyuktam arśovyādhir vināśayet ||10|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātamūtrapurīṣāṇi krimayaḥ śukram eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhagandarāt prasravanti yasya taṃ parivarjayet ||11|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         praśūnanābhivṛṣaṇaṃ ruddhamūtraṃ ruganvitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         aśmarī kṣapayatyāśu sikatā śarkarānvitā ||12|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         garbhakoṣaparāsaṅgo makkallo yonisaṃvṛtiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hanyāt striyaṃ mūḍhagarbhe yathoktāś cāpy upadravāḥ ||13|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pārśvabhaṅgānnavidveṣaśophātīsārapīḍitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         viriktaṃ pūryamāṇaṃ ca varjayed udarārditam ||14|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.15">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yas tāmyati visañjñaś ca śete nipatito 'pi vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītārdito 'ntaruṣṇaś ca jvareṇa mriyate naraḥ ||15|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.16">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yo hṛṣṭaromā raktākṣo hṛdi saṅghātaśūlavān |
                        <caesura/>
                         nityaṃ vaktreṇa cocchvasyāttaṃ jvaro hanti mānavam ||16||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.17">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hikkāśvāsapipāsārtaṃ mūḍhaṃ vibhrāntalocanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         santatocchvāsinaṃ kṣīṇaṃ naraṃ kṣapayati jvaraḥ ||17|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āvilākṣaṃ pratāmyantaṃ nidrāyuktamatīva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīṇaśoṇitamāṃsaṃ ca naraṃ nāśayati jvaraḥ ||18|</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śvāsaśūlapipāsārtaṃ kṣīṇaṃ jvaranipīḍitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣeṇa naraṃ vṛddhamatīsāro vināśayet ||19|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śuklākṣamannadveṣṭāramūrdhvaśvāsanipīḍitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛcchreṇa bahu mehantaṃ yakṣmā hantīha mānavam ||20|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śvāsaśūlapipāsānnavidveṣagranthimūḍhatāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti durbalatvaṃ ca gulmino mṛtyumeṣyataḥ ||21|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.22">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ādhmātaṃ baddhaniṣyandaṃ chardihikkātṛḍanvitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         rujāśvāsasamāviṣṭaṃ vidradhirnāśayennaram ||22|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.23">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pāṇḍudantanakho yaś ca pāṇḍunetraś ca mānavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pāṇḍusaṅghātadarśī ca pāṇḍurogī vinaśyati ||23|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.24">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         lohitaṃ chardayed yas tu bahuśo lohitekṣaṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         raktānāṃ ca diśāṃ draṣṭā raktapittī vinaśyati ||24|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.25">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         avāṅmukhastūnmukho vā kṣīṇamāṃsabalo naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jāgariṣṇur asandeham unmādena vinaśyati ||25|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.26">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.33.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bahuśo 'pasmarantaṃ tu prakṣīṇaṃ calitabhruvam |
                        <caesura/>
                         netrābhyāṃ ca vikurvāṇam apasmāro vināśayet ||26|| </l>

                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne 'vāraṇīyo nāma
                        trayastriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||33|| </p>
                </div>
                <div n="34" type="adhyāya">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.34.1</label>
                         athāto yuktasenīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.2">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.34.2</label>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.34.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nṛpater yuktasenasya parānabhijigīṣataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhiṣajā rakṣaṇaṃ kāryaṃ yathā tadupadekṣyate ||3|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.34.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vijigīṣuḥ sahāmātyairyātrāyuktaḥ prayatnataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣitavyo viśeṣeṇa viṣād eva narādhipaḥ ||4|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.34.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         panthānam udakaṃ chāyāṃ bhaktaṃ yavasam indhanam | dūṣayantyarayastac ca
                        jānīyācchodhayettathā ||5|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.34.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya liṅgaṃ cikitsā ca kalpasthāne pravakṣyate
                        <caesura/>
                         ekottaraṃ mṛtyuśatam atharvāṇaḥ pracakṣate ||6|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.34.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatraikaḥ kālasaṃyuktaḥ śeṣā āgantavaḥ smṛtāḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣāgantujamṛtyubhyo rasamantraviśāradau ||7|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.34.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣetāṃ nṛpatiṃ nityaṃ yattau vaidyapurohitau
                        <caesura/>
                         brahmā vedāṅgam aṣṭāṅgam āyurvedam abhāṣata ||8|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.34.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         purohitamate tasmād varteta bhiṣag ātmavān
                        <caesura/>
                         saṅkaraḥ sarvavarṇānāṃ praṇāśo dharmakarmaṇām ||9|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.34.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prajānām api cocchittirnṛpavyasanahetutaḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         puruṣāṇāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ ca kevalaṃ tulyamūrtitā ||10|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.34.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ājñā tyāgaḥ kṣamā dhairyaṃ vikramaś cāpy amānuṣaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād devam ivābhīkṣṇaṃ vāṅmanaḥkarmabhiḥ śubhaiḥ ||11|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.34.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         cintayen nṛpatiṃ vaidyaḥ śreyāṃsīcchan vicakṣaṇaḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         skandhāvāre ca mahati rājagehādanantaram ||12|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.34.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavetsannihito vaidyaḥ sarvopakaraṇānvitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrasthamenaṃ dhvajavadyaśaḥkhyātisamucchritam ||13|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.34.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         upasarpantyamohena viṣaśalyāmayārditāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         svatantrakuśalo 'nyeṣu śāstrārtheṣv abahiṣkṛtaḥ ||14||</l>

                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyo vyādhyupasṛṣṭaś ca bheṣajaṃ paricārakaḥ ||15|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.16">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.20">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.21">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         samīkṣya dattaṃ kāle ca bheṣajaṃ pāda ucyate ||23||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.12ab">

                        tatrāṅgāny antarādhisakthibāhuśirāṃsi, tad avayavāḥ pratyaṅgānīti | tatra,
                        svair aṅgulaiḥ pādāṅguṣṭhapradeśinyau dvyaṅgulāyate ; pradeśinyāstu
                        madhyamānāmikākaniṣṭhikā yathottaraṃ pañcamabhāgahīnāḥ; caturaṅgulāyate
                        pañcāṅgulavistṛte</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.12cd">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.12cd</label>
                         prapadapādatale; pañcacaturaṅgulāyatavistṛtā pārṣṇiḥ; caturdaśāṅgulāyataḥ
                        pādaḥ; caturdaśāṅgulapariṇāhāni pādagulphajaṅghājānumadhyāni; aṣṭādaśāṅgulā
                        jaṅghā, jānūpariṣṭācca dvātriṃśadaṅgulam, ete pañcāśat; jaṅghāyāmasamāvūrū;
                        dvyaṅgulāni vṛṣaṇacibukadaśananāsāpuṭabhāgakarṇamūlabhrūnayanāntarāṇi;
                        caturaṅgulāni mehanavadanāntaranāsākarṇalalāṭagrīvocchrāyadṛṣṭyantarāṇi;
                        dvādaśāṅgulāni
                        bhagavistāramehananābhihṛdayagrīvāstanāntaramukhāyāmamaṇibandhaprakoṣṭhasthaulyāni;
                        indrabastipariṇāhāṃsapīṭhakūrparāntarāyāmaḥ ṣoḍaśāṅgulaḥ; caturviṃśatyaṅgulo
                        hastaḥ; dvātriṃśadaṅgulaparimāṇau bhujau; dvātriṃśatpariṇāhāvūrū;
                        maṇibandhakūrparāntaraṃ ṣoḍaśāṅgulaṃ; talaṃ ṣaṭcaturaṅgulāyāmavistāram;
                        aṅguṣṭhamūlapradeśinīśravaṇāpāṅgāntaramadhyamāṅgulyau pañcāṅgule;
                        ardhapañcāṅgule pradeśinyanāmike; sārdhatryaṅgulau kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhau;
                        caturviṃśativistārapariṇāhaṃ mukhagrīvaṃ; tribhāgāṅgulavistārā
                        nāsāpuṭamaryādā; nayanatribhāgapariṇāhā tārakā; navamastārakāṃśo dṛṣṭiḥ;
                        keśāntamastakāntaramekādaśāṅgulaṃ; mastakādavaṭukeśānto daśāṅgulaḥ;
                        karṇāvaṭvantaraṃ caturdaśāṅgulaṃ; puruṣoraḥpramāṇavistīrṇā strīśroṇiḥ;
                        aṣṭādaśāṅgulavistāramuraḥ; tatpramāṇā puruṣasya kaṭī; saviṃśamaṅgulaśataṃ
                        puruṣāyāma iti ||12|| </l>

                        vyādhiṃ jaghanyakālajāto vyādhirupasṛjati, sa tanmūla evopadravasañjñaḥ;
                        prākkevalo nāma yaḥ prāgevotpanno vyādhirapūrvarūpo 'nupadravaśca;

                        ekaḥ, vikriyām āpannas trividho bhavati- viṣamo vātena, tīkṣṇaḥ pittena,
                        mandaḥ śleṣmaṇā, caturthaḥ samaḥ sarvasāmyāditi | tatra, yo yathākālam
                        upayuktamannaṃ samyak pacati sa samaḥ, samairdoṣaiḥ; yaḥ kadācit samyak
                        pacati, kadācidādhmānaśūlodāvartātisārajaṭharagauravāntrakūjanapravāhaṇāni
                        kṛtvā, sa viṣamaḥ; yaḥ prabhūtam apy upayuktam annam āśu pacati sa tīkṣṇaḥ,
                        sa evābhivardhamāno 'tyagnirity ābhāṣyate, sa muhur muhuḥ prabhūtam apy
                        upayuktam annam āśutaraṃ pacati, pākānte ca galatālvoṣṭhaśoṣadāhasantāpā
                        ñjanayati;
                        yastvalpamapyupayuktamudaraśirogauravakāsaśvāsaprasekacchardigātrasadanāni
                        kṛtvā mahatā kālena pacati, sa mandaḥ ||24|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.29">

                        <caesura/>

                        bālāḥ | te trividhāḥ- kṣīrapāḥ, kṣīrānnādā, annādā iti | teṣu
                        saṃvatsaraparāḥ kṣīrapāḥ, dvisaṃvatsaraparāḥ kṣīrānnādāḥ, parato 'nnādā iti
                        | ṣoḍaśasaptatyor antare madhyaṃ vayaḥ | tasya vikalpo- vṛddhiḥ, yauvanaṃ,
                        sampūrṇatā, parihāṇiriti | tatra, āviṃśatervṛddhiḥ, ātriṃśato yauvanam,
                        ācatvāriṃśataḥ sarvadhātvindriyabalavīryasampūrṇatā, ata
                        ūrdhvamīṣatparihāṇiryāvat saptatiriti | saptaterūrdhvaṃ
                        kṣīyamāṇadhātvindriyabalavīryotsāhamahanyahani valīpalitakhālity ajuṣṭaṃ
                        kāsaśvāsaprabhṛtibhir upadravairabhibhūyamānaṃ sarvakriyāsvasamarthaṃ
                        jīrṇāgāramivābhivṛṣṭamavasīdantaṃ vṛddhamācakṣate ||29|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.32">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         agnikṣāravirekais tu bālavṛddhau vivarjayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatsādhyeṣu vikāreṣu mṛdvīṃ kuryāt kriyāṃ śanaiḥ ||32|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.33">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dehaḥ sthūlaḥ, kṛśo, madhya, iti prāgupadiṣṭaḥ ||33|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.34">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         karśayed bṛṃhayec cāpi sadā sthūlakṛśau narau |
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣaṇaṃ caiva madhyasya kurvīta satataṃ bhiṣak ||34|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.35">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         balam abhihitaguṇaṃ; daurbalyaṃ tu svabhāvadoṣajarādibhir avekṣitavyam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yasmād balavataḥ sarvakriyāpravṛttis tasmād balam eva pradhānam
                        adhikaraṇānām ||35|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.36">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.36</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kecit kṛśāḥ prāṇavantaḥ sthūlāś cālpabalā narāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt sthiratvaṃ vyāyāmairbalaṃ vaidyaḥ pratarkayet ||36|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.37">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sattvaṃ tu vyasanābhyudayakriyādisthāneṣv aviklavakaram ||37|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.38">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sattvavān sahate sarvaṃ saṃstabhyātmānamātmanā |
                        <caesura/>
                         rājasaḥ stabhyamāno 'nyaiḥ sahate naiva tāmasaḥ ||38|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.39">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sātmyāni tu deśakālajātyṛturogavyāyāmodakadivāsvapnarasaprabhṛtīni
                        prakṛtiviruddhāny api yāny abādhakarāṇi bhavanti ||39|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.40">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.40</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yo rasaḥ kalpate yasya sukhāyaiva niṣevitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyāyāmajātamanyadvā tat sātmyam iti nirdiśet ||40|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.41">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.41</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prakṛtiṃ bheṣajaṃ copariṣṭād vakṣyāmaḥ ||41|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.42">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.42</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         deśastvānūpo jāṅgalaḥ sādhāraṇa iti | tatra,
                        bahūdakanimnonnatanadīvarṣagahano mṛduśītānilo bahumahāparvatavṛkṣo
                        mṛdusukumāropacitaśarīramanuṣyaprāyaḥ kaphavātarogabhūyiṣṭhaś cānūpaḥ;
                        ākāśasamaḥ praviralālpakaṇṭakivṛkṣaprāyo 'lpavarṣaprasravaṇodapānodakaprāya
                        uṣṇadāruṇavātaḥ praviralālpaśailaḥ sthirakṛśaśarīramanuṣyaprāyo
                        vātapittarogabhūyiṣṭhaś ca jāṅgalaḥ; ubhayadeśalakṣaṇaḥ sādhāraṇa iti ||42|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.43">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.43</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra
                        <caesura/>
                         samāḥ sādhāraṇe yasmācchītavarṣoṣmamārutāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣāṇāṃ samatā jantostasmāt sādhāraṇo mataḥ ||43|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.44">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.44</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na tathā balavantaḥ syurjalajā vā sthalāhṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         svadeśe nicitā doṣā anyasmin kopam āgatāḥ ||44|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.45">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.45</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ucite vartamānasya nāsti deśakṛtaṃ bhayam | ૉ
                        <caesura/>
                         āhārasvapnaceṣṭādau taddeśasya guṇe sati ||45||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.46">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.46</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         deśaprakṛtisātmyartu viparīto 'cirotthitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sampattau bhiṣagādīnāṃ balasattvāyuṣāṃ tathā ||46||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.47">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.47</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kevalaḥ samadehāgneḥ sukhasādhyatamo gadaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ato 'nyathā tvasādhyaḥ syāt kṛcchro vyāmiśralakṣaṇaḥ ||47||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.48">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.48</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kriyāyās tu guṇālābhe kriyām anyāṃ prayojayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūrvasyāṃ śāntavegāyāṃ na kriyāsaṅkaro hitaḥ ||48|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.49">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.49</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         guṇālābhe 'pi sapadi yadi saiva kriyā hitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kartavyaiva tadā vyādhiḥ kṛcchrasādhyatamo yadi ||49|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.50">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.35.50</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ya evam enaṃ vidhim ekarūpaṃ bibharti kālādivaśena dhīmān |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa mṛtyupāśāñ jagato gadaughāñ chinatti bhaiṣajyaparaśvadhena ||50|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne āturopakramaṇīyo
                        nāma pañcatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||35|| </l>
                </div>

                <div n="36" type="adhyāya">
                    <!--<note xml:lang="en">There are large differences
                                    between the Ācārya 1931 and 1938 editions version of
                                    Cakrapāṇidatta's commentary on this adhyāya.</note>-->

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.1"> athāto bhūmipravibhāgīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.36.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śvabhraśarkarāśmaviṣamavalmīkaśmaśānāghātanadevatāyatanasikatābhir
                        anupahatāmanūṣarāmabhaṅgurāmadūrodakāṃ snigdhāṃ prarohavatīṃ mṛdvīṃ sthirāṃ
                        samāṃ kṛṣṇāṃ gaurīṃ lohitāṃ vā bhūmim auṣadhagrahaṇāya parīkṣeta | tasyāṃ
                        jātamapi kṛmiviṣaśastrātapapavanadahanatoyasambādhamārgairanupahatamekarasaṃ
                        puṣṭaṃ pṛthvavagāḍhamūlamudīcyāṃ cauṣadhamādadītetyeṣa bhūmiparīkṣāviśeṣaḥ
                        sāmānyaḥ ||3|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.36.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣatas tu tatra, aśmavatī sthirā gurvī śyāmā kṛṣṇā vā
                        sthūlavṛkṣaśasyaprāyā svaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā; snigdhā śītalā''sannodakā
                        snigdhaśasyatṛṇakomalavṛkṣaprāyā śuklā'mbuguṇabhūyiṣṭhā; nānāvarṇā
                        laghvaśmavatī praviralālpapāṇḍuvṛkṣaprarohā'gniguṇabhūyiṣṭhā; rūkṣā
                        bhasmarāsabhavarṇā tanuvṛkṣālparasakoṭaravṛkṣaprāyā'nilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā; mṛdvī
                        samā śvabhravatyavyaktarasajalā sarvato 'sāravṛkṣā mahāparvatavṛkṣaprāyā
                        śyāmā cākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā ||4|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.36.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atra kecid āhur ācāryāḥ- prāvṛḍvarṣāśaraddhemantavasantagrīṣmeṣu
                        yathāsaṅkhyaṃ mūlapatratvakkṣīrasāraphalānyādadīteti; tat tu na samyak,
                        saumyāgneyatvājjagataḥ | saumyāny auṣadhāni saumyeṣvṛtuṣvādadīta,
                        āgneyānyāgneyeṣu; evamavyāpannaguṇāni bhavanti | saumyāny auṣadhmani
                        saumyeṣvṛtuṣu gṛhītāni somaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau
                        jātānyatimadhurasnigdhaśītāni jāyante | etena śeṣaṃ vyākhyātam ||5|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.36.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra pṛthivyambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau jātāni virecanadravyāṇyādadīta ,
                        agnyākāśamārutaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ vamanadravyāṇi,
                        ubhayaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāmubhayatobhāgāni, ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ saṃśamanāni,
                        evaṃ balavattarāṇi bhavanti ||6|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.36.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvāṇyeva cābhinavāni, anyatra madhughṛtaguḍapippalīviḍaṅgebhyaḥ ||7||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.36.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viḍaṅgaṃ pippalī kṣaudraṃ sarpiś cāpy anavaṃ hitam | śeṣam anyatv abhinavaṃ
                        gṛhṇīyāddoṣavarjitam ||8|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.36.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         (sarvāṇyeva sakṣīrāṇi vīryavanti;) teṣāṃ
                        asampattāvatikrāntasaṃvatsarāṇyādadīteti ||9|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.36.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra- gopālāstāpasā vyādhā ye cānye vanacāriṇaḥ | mūlāhārāś ca ye
                        tebhyo bheṣajavyaktiriṣyate ||10|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.36.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvāvayavasādhyeṣu palāśalavaṇādiṣu | vyavasthito na kālo 'sti tatra sarvo
                        vidhīyate ||11|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.36.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gandhavarṇarasopetā ṣaḍvidhā bhūmiriṣyate | tasmād bhūmisvabhāvena bījinaḥ
                        ṣaḍrasāyutāḥ ||12|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.36.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         avyaktaḥ kila toyasya raso niścayaniścitaḥ | rasaḥ sa eva cāvyakto vyakto
                        bhūmirasādbhavet ||13|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.36.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvalakṣaṇasampannā bhūmiḥ sādhāraṇā smṛtā | dravyāṇi yatra tatraiva
                        tadguṇāni viśeṣataḥ ||14|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.15">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.36.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vigandhenāparāmṛṣṭamavipannaṃ rasādibhiḥ | navaṃ dravyaṃ purāṇaṃ vā
                        grāhyamevaṃ vinirdiśet ||15|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.16">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.36.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jaṅgamānāṃ vayaḥsthānāṃ raktaromanakhādikam | kṣīramūtrapurīṣāṇi
                        jīrṇāhāreṣu saṃharet ||16|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.17">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.36.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         plotamṛdbhāṇḍaphalakaśaṅkuvinyastabheṣajam | praśastāyāṃ diśi śucau
                        bheṣajāgāramiṣyate ||17|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.trailer">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.36.trailer</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne bhūmipravibhāgīyo nāma ṣaṭtriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
                        ||36|| </l>
                </div>
                <div n="37" type="adhyāya">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto miśrakam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.2">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mātuluṅgyagnimanthau ca bhadradāru mahauṣadham |
                        <caesura/>
                         ahiṃsrā caiva rāsnā ca pralepo vātaśophajit ||3|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dūrvā ca nalamūlaṃ ca madhukaṃ candanaṃ tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītalāśca gaṇāḥ sarve pralepaḥ pittaśophahṛt ||4|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āgantuje raktaje ca hyeṣa eva vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidhir viṣaghno viṣaje pittaghno 'pi hitas tathā ||5|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ajagandhā'śvagandhā ca kālā saralayā saha |
                        <caesura/>
                         ekaiṣikājaśṛṅgī ca pralepaḥ śleṣmaśophahṛt ||6|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ete vargās trayo lodhraṃ pathyā piṇḍītakāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         anantā ceti lepo 'yaṃ sānnipātikaśophahṛt ||7|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdhāmlalavaṇo vāte koṣṇaḥ, śītaḥ payoyutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pitte, coṣṇaḥ kaphe kṣāramūtrāḍhyastatpraśāntaye ||8|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śaṇamūlakaśigrūṇāṃ phalāni tilasarṣapāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saktavaḥ kiṇvamatasī dravyāṇyuṣṇāni pācanam ||9|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         cirabilvo 'gniko dantī citrako hayamārakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kapotakaṅkagṛdhrāṇāṃ purīṣāṇi ca dāraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣāradravyāṇi vā yāni kṣāro vā dāraṇaṃ param ||10|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dravyāṇāṃ picchilānāṃ tu tvaṅmūlāni prapīḍanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yavagodhūmamāṣāṇāṃ cūrṇāni ca samāsataḥ ||11|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śāṅkhinyaṅkoṭhasumanaḥkaravīrasuvarcalāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhanāni kaṣāyāṇi vargaś cāragvadhādikaḥ ||12|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ajagandhā'jaśṛṅgī ca gavākṣī lāṅgalāhvayā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūtīkaś citrakaḥ pāṭhā viḍaṅgailāhareṇavaḥ ||13|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yavakṣāro lavaṇāni manaḥśilā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāsīsaṃ trivṛtā dantī haritālaṃ surāṣṭrajā ||14||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.15">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃśodhanīnāṃ vartīnāṃ dravyāṇy etāni nirdiśet
                        <caesura/>
                         etair eva uṣadhaiḥ kuryāt kalkānapi ca śodhanān ||15|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.16">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         arkottamāṃ snuhīkṣīraṃ piṣṭvā kṣārottamāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         jātīmūlaṃ haridre dve kāsīsaṃ kaṭurohiṇīm ||16|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.17">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pūrvoddiṣṭāni cānyāni kuryāt saṃśodhanaṃ ghṛtam
                        <caesura/>
                         mayūrako rājavṛkṣo nimbaḥ kośātakī tilāḥ ||17|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bṛhatī kaṇṭakārī ca haritālaṃ manaḥśilā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhanāni ca yojyāni taile dravyāṇi śodhane ||18||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kāsīse saindhave kiṇve vacāyāṃ rajanīdvaye |
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhanāṅgeṣu cānyeṣu cūrṇaṃ kurvīta śodhanam ||19|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sālasārādisāreṣu paṭolatriphalāsu ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasakriyā vidhātavyā śodhanī śodhaneṣu ca ||20|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śrīveṣṭake sarjarase sarale devadāruṇi |
                        <caesura/>
                         sāreṣv api ca kurvīta matimān vraṇadhūpanam ||21|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.22">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyāṇāmanuṣṇānāṃ vṛkṣāṇāṃ tvakṣu sādhitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śṛtaḥ śītakaṣāyo vā ropaṇārthaṃ praśasyate ||22|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.23">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         somāmṛtāśvagandhāsu kākolyādau gaṇe tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīripraroheṣv api ca vartayo ropaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ||23|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.24">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         samaṅgā somasaralā somavalkaḥ sacandanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kākolyādiś ca kalkaḥ syāt praśasto vraṇaropaṇe ||24|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.25">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pṛthakparṇyātmaguptā ca haridre mālatī sitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kākolyādiś ca yojyaḥ syādbhiṣajā ropaṇe ghṛte ||25|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.26">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kālānusāryāguruṇī haridre devadāru ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         priyaṅgavaśca rodhraṃ ca taile yojyāni ropaṇe ||26|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.27">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṅgukā triphalā rodhraṃ kāsīsaṃ śravaṇāhvayā |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhavāśvakarṇayos tvak ca ropaṇaṃ cūrṇamiṣyate ||27|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.28">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         priyaṅgukā sarjarasaḥ puṣpakāsīsam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tvakcūrṇaṃ dhavajaṃ caiva ropaṇārthaṃ praśasyate ||28|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.29">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tvakṣu nyagrodhavargasya triphalāyās tathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasakriyāṃ ropaṇārthe vidadhīta yathākramam ||29|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.30">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         apāmārgo 'śvagandhā ca tālapatrī suvarcalā |
                        <caesura/>
                         utsādane praśasyante kākolyādiś ca yo gaṇaḥ ||30|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.31">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kāsīsaṃ saindhavaṃ kiṇvaṃ kuruvindo manaḥśilā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kukkuṭāṇḍakapālāni sumanomukulāni ca ||31|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.32">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         phale śairīṣakārañje dhātucūrṇāni yāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇeṣūtsannamāṃseṣu praśastānyavasādane ||32||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.33">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         samastaṃ vargamardhaṃ vā yathālābhamathāpi vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         prayuñjīta bhiṣak prājño yathoddiṣṭeṣu karmasu ||33|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.trailer">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.37.trailer</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne miśrakādhyāyo nāma saptatriṃśattamo
                        'dhyāyaḥ ||37|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākavijñānīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.2">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kecid ācāryā bruvate- dravyaṃ pradhānaṃ, kasmāt? vyavasthitatvāt , iha
                        khalu dravyaṃ vyavasthitaṃ na rasādayaḥ, yathā āme phale ye rasādayaste
                        pakve na santi; nity atvācca, nityaṃ hi dravyamanity ā guṇāḥ, yathā
                        kalkādipravibhāgaḥ, sa eva sampannarasagandho vyāpannarasagandho vā bhavati;
                        svajātyavasthānācca, yathā hi pārthivaṃ dravyamanyabhāvaṃ na gacchaty evaṃ
                        śeṣāṇi; pañcendriyagrahaṇāśca, pañcabhir indriyairgṛhyate dravyaṃ na
                        rasādayaḥ; āśrayatvācca, dravyamāśritā rasādayaḥ; ārambhasāmarthyācca,
                        dravyāśrita ārambhaḥ, yathā- ‘vidārigandhādimāhṛtya saṅkṣudya vipacet’ ity
                        evam ādiṣu na rasādiṣvārambhaḥ; śāstraprāmāṇyācca, śāstre hi dravyaṃ
                        pradhānam upadeśe yogānāṃ, yathā- ‘mātuluṅgāgnimanthau ca’ ity ādau na
                        rasādaya upadiśyante; kramāpekṣitatvācca rasādīnāṃ, rasādayo hi
                        dravyakramamapekṣante, yathā- taruṇe taruṇāḥ sampūrṇe sampūrṇā iti;
                        ekadeśasādhyatvācca, dravyāṇāmekadeśenāpi vyādhayaḥ sādhyante, yathā-
                        mahāvṛkṣakṣīreṇeti; tasmād dravyaṃ pradhānaṃ, na rasādayaḥ, kasmāt?
                        niravayavatvāt | dravyalakṣaṇaṃ tu ‘kriyāguṇavat samavāyikāraṇam’ iti ||3|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         netyāhuranye , rasās tu pradhānaṃ; kasmāt? āgamāt, āgamo hi śāstramucyate;
                        śāstre hi rasā adhikṛtāḥ, yathā- rasāyatta āhāra iti, tasmiṃs tu prāṇāḥ;
                        upadeśācca, upadiśyante hi rasāḥ, yathā- madhurāmlalavaṇā vātaṃ śamayanti;
                        anumānācca, rasena hy anumīyate dravyaṃ, yathā- madhuramiti; ṛṣivacanācca,
                        ṛṣivacanaṃ vedo yathā- kiñcidijyārthaṃ madhuramāharediti, tasmād rasāḥ
                        pradhānaṃ; raseṣu guṇasañjñā | rasalakṣaṇamanyatropadekṣyāmaḥ ||4|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nety āhur anye , vīryaṃ pradhānam iti | kasmāt? tad
                        vaśenauṣadhakarmaniṣpatteḥ |
                        ihauṣadhakarmāṇyūrdhvādhobhāgobhayabhāgasaṃśodhanasaṃśamanasaṅgrāhikāgnidīpanapīḍanalekhanabṛṃhaṇa-
                        rasāyanavājīkaraṇaśvayathukaravilayanadahanadāraṇamādanaprāṇaghnaviṣapraśamanādīni
                        vīryaprādhānyādbhavanti | tac ca vīryaṃ dvividhamuṣṇaṃ śītaṃ ca,
                        agnīṣomīyatvājjagataḥ | kecid aṣṭavidhamāhuḥ- śītamuṣṇaṃ snigdhaṃ rūkṣaṃ
                        viśadaṃ picchilaṃ mṛdu tīkṣṇaṃ ceti | etāni vīryāṇi
                        svabalaguṇotkarṣādrasamabhibhūyātmakarma kurvanti | yathā
                        tāvanmahatpañcamūlaṃ kaṣāyaṃ tiktānurasaṃ vātaṃ śamayati, uṣṇavīryatvāt ;
                        tathā kulatthaḥ kaṣāyaḥ, kaṭukaḥ palāṇḍuḥ, snehabhāvācca; madhuraścekṣuraso
                        vātaṃ vardhayati, śītavīryatvāt ; kaṭukā pippalī pittaṃ śamayati,
                        mṛduśītavīryatvāt ; amlamāmalakaṃ lavaṇaṃ saindhavaṃ ca; tiktā kākamācī
                        pittaṃ vardhayati, uṣṇavīryatvāt , madhurā matsyāśca; kaṭukaṃ mūlakaṃ
                        śleṣmāṇaṃ vardhayati, snigdhavīryatvāt ; amlaṃ kapitthaṃ śleṣmāṇāṃ śamayati,
                        rūkṣavīryatvāt , madhuraṃ kṣaudraṃ ca; tad etan nidarśanamātram uktam ||5|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra
                        <caesura/>
                         ye rasā vātaśamanā bhavanti yadi teṣu vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         raukṣyalāghavaśaity āni na te hanyuḥ samīraṇam ||6|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ye rasāḥ pittaśamanā bhavanti yadi teṣu vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         taikṣṇyauṣṇyalaghutāś caiva na te tat karmakāriṇaḥ ||7|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ye rasāḥ śleṣmaśamanā bhavanti yadi teṣu vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehagauravaśaityāni na te tatkarmakāriṇaḥ ||8||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād vīryaṃ pradhānam iti ||9||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nety āhur anye , vipākaḥ pradhānam iti | kasmāt? samyaṅmithyāvipakvatvāt ;
                        iha sarvadravāṇyabhyavahṛtāni samyaṅmithyāvipakvāni guṇaṃ doṣaṃ vā janayanti
                        | tatrāhuranye- prati rasaṃ pāka iti | kecittrividhamicchanti- madhuramamlaṃ
                        kaṭukaṃ ceti | tat tu na samyak, bhūtaguṇādāmāccānyo 'mlo vipāko nāsti;
                        pittaṃ hi vidagdhamamlatām upaity āgneyatvāt ; yadyevaṃ lavaṇo 'pyanyaḥ pāko
                        bhaviṣyati, śleṣmā hi vidagdho lavaṇatām upaitīti | madhuro madhurasyāmlo
                        'mlasyaivaṃ sarveṣām iti kecidāhuḥ; dṛṣṭāntaṃ copadiśanti- yathā tāvat
                        kṣīramukhāgataṃ pacyamānaṃ madhuram eva syāttathā śāliyavamudgādayaḥ
                        prakīrṇāḥ svabhāvamuttarakāle 'pi na parity ajanti tadvaditi | kecidvadanti-
                        abalavanto balavatāṃ vaśamāyāntīti | evamanavasthitiḥ, tasmād asiddhānta
                        eṣaḥ | āgame hi dvividha eva pāko madhuraḥ kaṭukaś ca | tayor madhurākhyo
                        guruḥ, kaṭukākhyo laghuriti | tatra pṛthivyaptejovāyvākāśānāṃ dvaividhyaṃ
                        bhavati guṇasādharmyād gurutā laghutā ca; pṛthivyāpaś ca gurvyaḥ, śeṣāṇi
                        laghūni; tasmād dvividha eva pāka iti ||10|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra
                        <caesura/>
                         dravyeṣu pacyamāneṣu yeṣv ambupṛthivīguṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nirvartante 'dhikās tatra pāko madhura ucyate ||11||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tejo 'nilākāśaguṇāḥ pacyamāneṣu yeṣu tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         nirvartante 'dhikās tatra pākaḥ kaṭuka ucyate ||12|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pṛthaktvadarśināmeṣa vādināṃ vādasaṅgrahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         caturṇāmapi sāmagryam icchanty atra vipaścitaḥ ||13|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tad dravyam ātmanā kiñcit kiñcid vīryeṇa sevitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kiñcid rasavipākābhyāṃ doṣaṃ hanti karoti vā ||14|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.15">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pāko nāsti vinā vīryādvīryaṃ nāsti vinā rasāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         raso nāsti vinā dravyāddravyaṃ śreṣṭhatamaṃ smṛtam ||15|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.16">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         janma tu dravyarasayor anyonyāpekṣikaṃ smṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         anyonyāpekṣikaṃ janma yathā syād dehadehinoḥ ||16|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.17">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vīryasañjñā guṇā ye 'ṣṭau te 'pi dravyāśrayāḥ smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         raseṣu na bhavanty ete nirguṇās tu guṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ||17||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dravye dravyāṇi yasmāddhi vipacyante na ṣaḍrasāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śreṣṭhaṃ dravyamato jñeyaṃ, śeṣā bhāvās tad āśrayāḥ ||18|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         amīmāṃsyāny acintyāni prasiddhāni svabhāvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āgamenopayojyāni bheṣajāni vicakṣaṇaiḥ ||19|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pratyakṣalakṣaṇaphalāḥ prasiddhāś ca svabhāvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nauṣadhīrhetubhir vidvān parīkṣeta kadācana ||20|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.40.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sahasreṇāpi hetūnāṃ nāmbaṣṭhādir virecayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt tiṣṭhet tu matimān āgame na tu hetuṣu ||21|| </l>

                        śabdasparśarūparasagandhāḥ, tasmād āpyo rasaḥ | parasparasaṃsargāt
                        parasparānugrahāt parasparānupraveśāc ca sarveṣu sarveṣāṃ sānnidhyamasti,

                        gauravād gauravaṃ, śaityāc chaity aṃ, paicchilyāt paicchilyam iti (3) ||8|| </l>

                        chaityaṃ, vaiśadyāt paicchilyam iti | tad etan nidarśanamātram uktaṃ bhavati
                        (4) ||8|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.42.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasalakṣaṇam ata ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ- tatra, yaḥ paritoṣamutpādayati
                        prahlādayati tarpayati jīvayati mukhopalepaṃ janayati śleṣmāṇaṃ
                        cābhivardhayati sa madhuraḥ; yo dantaharṣam utpādayati mukhāsrāvaṃ janayati
                        śraddhāṃ cotpādayati so 'mlaḥ; yo bhaktarucim utpādayati kaphaprasekaṃ
                        janayati mārdavaṃ cāpādayati sa lavaṇaḥ; yo jihvāgraṃ bādhate udvegaṃ
                        janayati śiro gṛhṇīte nāsikāṃ srāvayati sa kaṭukaḥ; yo gale coṣamutpādayati
                        mukhavaiśadyaṃ janayati bhaktaruciṃ cāpādayati harṣaṃ ca sa tiktaḥ; yo
                        vaktraṃ pariśoṣayati jihvāṃ stambhayati kaṇṭhaṃ badhnāti hṛdayaṃ karṣati
                        pīḍayati ca sa kaṣāya iti ||9|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.42.10.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasaguṇān ata ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ- tatra, madhuro raso rasaraktamāṃsamedo
                        'sthimajjaujaḥśukrastanyavardhanaś cakṣuṣyaḥ keśyo varṇyo balakṛtsandhānaḥ
                        śoṇitarasaprasādano bālavṛddhakṣatakṣīṇahitaḥ
                        ṣaṭpadapipīlikānāmiṣṭatamastṛṣṇāmūrcchādāhapraśamanaḥ ṣaḍindriyaprasādanaḥ
                        kṛmikaphakaraś ceti; sa evaṅguṇo 'pyeka evātyartham āsevyamānaḥ
                        kāsaśvāsālasakavamathuvadanamādhuryasvaropaghātakṛmigalagaṇḍānāpādayati
                        tathā'rbudaślīpadabastigudopalepābhiṣyandaprabhṛtī ñjanayati(1) |10| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.2">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.42.10.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         amlo jaraṇaḥ pācano dīpanaḥ pavananigrahaṇo 'nulomanaḥ koṣṭhavidāhī
                        bahiḥśītaḥ kledanaḥ prāyaśo hy adyaśceti; sa evaṅguṇo 'pyeka evātyartham
                        upasevyamāno
                        dantaharṣanayanasammīlanaromasaṃvejanakaphavilayanaśarīraśaithilyānyāpādayati,
                        tathā
                        kṣatābhihatadagdhadaṣṭabhagnarugṇaśūnapracyutāvamūtritavisarpitacchinnabhinnaviddhotpiṣṭādīni
                        pācayatyāgneyasvabhāvāt paridahati kaṇṭhamuro hṛdayaṃ ceti(2) |10|</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.42.10.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         lavaṇaḥ saṃśodhanaḥ pācano viśleṣaṇaḥ kledanaḥ śaithilyakṛduṣṇaḥ
                        sarvarasapratyanīko mārgaviśodhanaḥ sarvaśarīrāvayavamārdavakaraśceti; sa
                        evaṅguṇo 'pyeka evātyarthamāsevyamāno
                        gātrakaṇḍūkoṭhaśophavaivarṇyapuṃstvopaghātendriyopatāpamukhākṣipākaraktapittavātaśoṇitāmlīkāprabhṛtīn
                        āpādayati(3) |10| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.42.10.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṭuko dīpanaḥ pācano rocanaḥ śodhanaḥ
                        sthaulyālasyakaphakṛmiviṣakuṣṭhakaṇḍūpraśamanaḥ sandhibandhavicchedano
                        'vasādanaḥ stanyaśukramedasām upahantā ceti; sa evaṅguṇo 'pyeka evātyartham
                        upasevyamāno
                        bhramamadagalatālvoṣṭhaśoṣadāhasantāpabalavighātakampatodabhedakṛt
                        karacaraṇapārśvapṛṣṭhaprabhṛtiṣu ca vātaśūlān āpādayati(4) |10|</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.42.10.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tiktaśchedano rocano dīpanaḥ śodhanaḥ kaṇḍūkoṭhatṛṣṇāmūrcchājvarapraśamanaḥ
                        stanyaśodhano viṇmūtrakledamedovasāpūyopaśoṣaṇaśceti; sa evaṅguṇo 'pyeka
                        evātyartham upasevyamāno
                        gātramanyāstambhākṣepakārditaśiraḥśūlabhramatodabhedacchedāsyavairasyāny
                        āpādayati(5) |10| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.42.10.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyaḥ saṅgrāhako ropaṇaḥ stambhanaḥ śodhano lekhanaḥ śoṣaṇaḥ pīḍanaḥ
                        kledopaśoṣaṇaś ceti; sa evaṅguṇo 'pyeka evātyartham upasevyamāno
                        hṛtpīḍāsyaśoṣodarādhmānavākyagrahamanyāstambha-
                        gātrasphuraṇacumucumāyanākuñcanākṣepaṇaprabhṛtī ñjanayati ||10|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.42.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ataḥ sarveṣām eva dravyāṇyupadekṣyāmaḥ | tad yathā- kākolyādiḥ
                        kṣīraghṛtavasāmajjaśāliṣaṣṭikayavagodhūmamāṣaśṛṅgāṭakakaserukatrapusair
                        vārukarkārukālābūkālindakataka-
                        giloḍyapriyālapuṣkarabījakāśmaryamadhūkadrākṣākharjūrarājādanatālanālikerekṣuvikārabalātibalātmaguptā-
                        vidārīpayasyāgokṣurakakṣīramoraṭamadhūlikākūṣmāṇḍaprabhṛtīni samāsena
                        madhuro vargaḥ;
                        dāḍimāmalakamātuluṅgāmrātakakapitthakaramardabadarakolaprācīnāmalakatintiḍīkakośāmrakabhavyapārāvata-
                        vetraphalalakucāmlavetasadantaśaṭhadadhitakrasurāśuktasauvīrakatuṣodakadhānyāmlaprabhṛtīni
                        samāsenāmlo vargaḥ;
                        saindhavasauvarcalaviḍapākyaromakasāmudrakapaktrimayavakṣāroṣaraprasūtasuvarcikāprabhṛtīni
                        samāsena lavaṇo vargaḥ; pippalyādiḥ surasādiḥ
                        śigrumadhuśigrumūlakalaśunasumukhaśītaśivakuṣṭhadevadāruhareṇukāvālgujaphala-
                        caṇḍāguggulumustalāṅgalakīśukanāsāpīluprabhṛtīni sālasārādiś ca prāyaśaḥ
                        kaṭuko vargaḥ;
                        āragvadhādirguḍūcyādirmaṇḍūkaparṇīvetrakarīraharidrādvayendrayavavaruṇasvādukaṇṭakasaptaparṇabṛhatīdvayaśaṅkhinīdravantī-
                        trivṛtkṛtavedhanakarkoṭakakāravellavārtākakarīrakaravīrasumanaḥśaṅkhapuṣpyapāmārgatrāyamāṇāśokarohiṇīvaijayantī-
                        suvarcalāpunarnavāvṛścikālījyotiṣmatīprabhṛtīni samāsena tikto vargaḥ;
                        nyagrodhādirambaṣṭhādiḥ priyaṅgvādī
                        rodhrādistriphalāśallakījambvāmrabakulatindukaphalāni
                        katakaśākaphalapāṣāṇabhedakavanaspatiphalāni sālasārādiś ca prāyaśaḥ
                        kuruvakakovidārakajīvantīcillīpālaṅkyāsuniṣaṇṇakaprabhṛtīni varakādayo
                        mudgādayaś ca samāsena kaṣāyo vargaḥ ||11|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.42.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatraiteṣāṃ rasānāṃ saṃyogāstriṣaṣṭirbhavanti | tad yathā- pañcadaśa
                        dvikāḥ, viṃśatistrikāḥ, pañcadaśa catuṣkāḥ, ṣaṭ pañcakāḥ, ekaśaḥ ṣaḍrasāḥ,
                        ekaḥ ṣaṭka iti | teṣāṃ anyatra prayojanāni vakṣyāmaḥ ||12|| </l>

                        <caesura/>
                         vamanadravyāṇāṃ phalādīnāṃ madanaphalāni śreṣṭhatamāni bhavanti | atha
                        madanapuṣpāṇāmātapapariśuṣkāṇāṃ cūrṇaprakuñjaṃ
                        pratyakpuṣpāsadāpuṣpīnimbakaṣāyāṇāmanyatamenāloḍya madhusaindhavayuktāṃ
                        puṣpacūrṇamātrāṃ pāyayitvā vāmayet | madanaśalāṭucūrṇānyevaṃ vā
                        bakularamyakopayuktāni madhulavaṇayuktānyabhiprataptāni;
                        madanaśalāṭucūrṇasiddhāṃ vā tilataṇḍulayavāgūm | nirvṛttānāṃ vā
                        nātiharitapāṇḍūnāṃ kuśamūḍhāvabaddhamṛdgomayapraliptānāṃ
                        yavabu(tu)ṣamudgamāṣaśālyādidhānyarāśāvaṣṭarātroṣitaklinnabhinnānāṃ phalānāṃ
                        phalapippalīruddhṛtyātape śoṣayet, tāsāṃ
                        dadhimadhupalalavimṛditapariśuṣkāṇāṃ subhājanasthānāmantarnakhamuṣṭimuṣṇe
                        yaṣṭīmadhukakaṣāye kovidārādīnāmanyatame vā kaṣāye pramṛdya rātriparyuṣitaṃ
                        madhusaindhavayuktamāśīrbhir abhimantritamudaṅmukhaḥ prāṅmukhamāturaṃ
                        pāyayed anena mantreṇābhimantrya-</l>

                        pravartayed āsamyagvāntalakṣaṇād iti | madanaphalamajjacūrṇaṃ vā

                        payasaḥ santānikāṃ kṣaudrayuktāṃ , madanaphalamajjasiddhaṃ vā payaḥ,
                        madanaphalamajjasiddhena vā payasā yavāgūm, adhobhāgāsṛkpittahṛddāhayoḥ;
                        madanaphalamajjasiddhasya vā payaso dadhibhāvam upagatasya dadhyuttaraṃ
                        dadhi vā kaphaprasekacchardimūrcchātamakeṣu; madanaphalamajjarasaṃ snehaṃ vā
                        bhallātakasnehavadādāya phāṇitībhūtaṃ lehayet, ātapapariśuṣkaṃ vā tam eva
                        jīvantīkaṣāyeṇa, pitte kaphasthānagate; madanaphalamajjakvāthaṃ vā
                        pippalyādipratīvāpaṃ, taccūrṇaṃ vā nimbarūpikākaṣāyayor anyatareṇa

                        dhāraṇamāśvāsajananaṃ
                        śramaklamapipāsāmadamūrcchātandrānidrādāhapraśamanamekāntataḥ pathyatamaṃ ca
                        ||3|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.45.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tad evāvanipatitam anyatamaṃ rasam upalabhate sthānaviśeṣān
                        nadīnadasarastaḍāgavāpīkūpacuṇṭīprasravaṇodbhidavikirakedārapalvalādiṣu
                        sthāneṣv avasthitam iti ||4|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.5">

                        madhurāmlalavaṇakaṭutiktakaṣāyāṇi yathāsaṅkhyam udakāni sambhavanti’ ity eke
                        bhāṣante ||5|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.45.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tat tu na samyak pṛthivyādīnām anyonyānupraveśakṛtaḥ salilaraso bhavaty
                        utkarṣāpakarṣeṇa | tatra, svalakṣaṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmāv amlaṃ lavaṇaṃ ca
                        ambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ madhuraṃ; tejoguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ kaṭukaṃ tiktaṃ ca
                        vāyuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ kaṣāyam; ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām avyaktarasam, avyaktaṃ
                        hy ākāśam ity ataḥ; tat pradhānam avyaktarasatvāt tat peyam āntarīkṣālābhe
                        ||6|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.45.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrāntarīkṣaṃ caturvidham | tad yathā dhāraṃ, kāraṃ, tauṣāraṃ, haimam iti
                        | teṣāṃ dhāraṃ pradhānaṃ, laghutvāt ; tat punardvividhaṃ- gāṅgaṃ, sāmudraṃ
                        ceti | tatra gāṅgamāśvayuje māsi prāyaśo varṣati | tayor dvayor api
                        parīkṣaṇaṃ kurvīta- śālyodanapiṇḍamakuthitamavidagdhaṃ rajatabhājanopahitaṃ
                        varṣati deve bahiṣkurvīta, sa yadi muhūrtaṃ sthitastādṛśa eva bhavati tadā
                        gāṅgaṃ patatītyavagantavyaṃ; varṇānyatve sikthapraklede ca sāmudram iti
                        vidyāt, tannopādeyam | sāmudramapyāśvayuje māsi gṛhītaṃ gāṅgavadbhavati |
                        gāṅgaṃ punaḥ pradhānaṃ, tadupādadītāśvayuje māsi |
                        śuciśuklavitatapaṭaikadeśacyutamathavā harmyatalaparibhraṣṭamanyair vā
                        śucibhir bhājanairgṛhītaṃ sauvarṇe rājate mṛnmaye vā pātre nidadhyāt | tat
                        sarvakālam upayuñjīta, tasyālābhe bhaumam | taccākāśaguṇabahulam | tat punaḥ
                        saptavidham | tad yathā- kaupaṃ, nādeyaṃ, sārasaṃ, tāḍāgaṃ, prāsravaṇam,
                        audbhidaṃ, cauṇṭyam iti ||7|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.8">

                        prasannatvāt hemante sārasaṃ tāḍāgaṃ vā; vasante kaupaṃ prāsravaṇaṃ vā;
                        grīṣme 'pyevaṃ; prāvṛṣi cauṇṭyamanabhivṛṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ ceti ||8|| </l>

                        vidyāt | tasya sparśarūparasagandhavīryavipākadoṣāḥ ṣaṭ sambhavanti | tatra,
                        kharatā paicchilyam auṣṇyaṃ dantagrāhitā ca sparśadoṣaḥ,

                        aniṣṭagandhatā gandhadoṣaḥ; yad upayuktaṃ tṛṣṇāgauravaśūlakaphaprasekān

                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.45.218</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavataś cātra
                        <caesura/>
                         tat sarvaṃ kaṭu tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ lavaṇānurasaṃ laghu |
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhanaṃ kaphavātaghnaṃ kṛmimedoviṣāpaham ||218|| </l>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.220">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.229">

                        <caesura/>

                        'dhyāyaḥ ||45|| </l>

                <div n="46" type="adhyāya">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.1</label>
                         athāto 'nnapānavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.2">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.2</label>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhanvantarim abhivādya suśruta uvāca- prāgabhihitaḥ ‘prāṇināṃ
                        punarmūlamāhāro balavarṇaujasāṃ ca, sa ṣaṭsu raseṣvāyattaḥ, rasāḥ
                        punardravyāśrayiṇaḥ,’ dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākanimitte ca kṣayavṛddhī
                        doṣāṇāṃ sāmyaṃ ca, brahmāderapi ca lokasyāhāraḥ sthity utpattivināśahetuḥ,
                        āhārādevābhivṛddhirbalamārogyaṃ varṇendriyaprasādaśca, tathā
                        hyāhāravaiṣamyādasvāsthyaṃ; tasyāśitapītalīḍhakhāditasya
                        nānādravyātmakasyānekavidhavikalpasyānekavidhaprabhāvasya pṛthak
                        pṛthagdravyarasaguṇavīryavipākakarmāṇīcchāmi jñātuṃ, na hy
                        anavabuddhasvabhāvā bhiṣajaḥ svasthānuvṛttiṃ roganigrahaṇaṃ ca kartuṃ
                        samarthāḥ; āhārāyattāś ca sarvaprāṇino yasmāttasmād annapānavidhim upadiśatu
                        me bhagavānity uktaḥ provāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ- atha khalu vatsa
                        suśruta! yathāpraśnamucyamānam upadhārayasva- ||3|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra,
                        lohitaśālikalamakardamakapāṇḍukasugandhakaśakunāhṛtapuṣpāṇḍakapuṇḍarīkamahāśāliśītabhīrukarodhrapuṣpaka-
                        dīrghaśūkakāñcanakamahiṣamahāśūkahāyanakadūṣakamahādūṣakaprabhṛtayaḥ śālayaḥ
                        ||4|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.47">

                        <caesura/>
                         jñeyā vipāke madhurā rase ca balapradāḥ pittanibarhaṇāś ca
                        <caesura/>

                         sudurjaraḥ svāduraso bṛṃhaṇastaṇḍulo navaḥ ||416|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.417">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.418">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.419">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         tathāmlayoge madhureṇa tṛptās teṣāṃ yatheṣṭaṃ pravadanti pathyam ||419|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.420">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.422">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.423">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.433">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.433</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra pūrvaśasyajātānāṃ badarāmlaṃ, vaidalānāṃ dhānyāmlaṃ, jaṅghālānāṃ
                        dhanvajānāṃ ca pippalyāsavaḥ, viṣkirāṇāṃ kolabadarāsavaḥ, pratudānāṃ
                        kṣīravṛkṣāsavaḥ, guhāśayānāṃ kharjūranālikerāsavaḥ,
                        prasahānāmaśvagandhāsavaḥ, parṇamṛgāṇāṃ kṛṣṇagandhāsavaḥ, bileśayānāṃ
                        phalāsavaḥ , ekaśaphānāṃ triphalāsavaḥ, anekaśaphānāṃ khadirāsavaḥ,
                        kūlacarāṇāṃ śṛṅgāṭakakaśerukāsavaḥ, kośavāsināṃ pādināṃ ca sa eva,
                        plavānāmikṣurasāsavaḥ, nādeyānāṃ matsyānāṃ mṛṇālāsavaḥ, sāmudrāṇāṃ
                        mātuluṅgāsavaḥ, amlānāṃ phalānāṃ padmotpalakandāsavaḥ, kaṣāyāṇāṃ
                        dāḍimavetrāsavaḥ, madhurāṇāṃ trikaṭukayuktaḥ khaṇḍāsavaḥ, tālaphalādīnāṃ
                        dhānyāmlaṃ, kaṭukānāṃ dūrvānalavetrāsavaḥ, pippalyādīnāṃ
                        śvadaṃṣṭrāvasukāsavaḥ, kūṣmāṇḍādīnāṃ dārvīkarīrāsavaḥ, cuccuprabhṛtīnāṃ
                        lodhrāsavaḥ, jīvantyādīnāṃ triphalāsavaḥ, kusumbhaśākasya sa eva,
                        maṇḍūkaparṇyādīnāṃ mahāpañcamūlāsavaḥ, tālamastakādīnāmamlaphalāsavaḥ,
                        saindhavādīnāṃ surāsava āranālaṃ ca, toyaṃ vā sarvatreti ||433|| </l>

                        <caesura/>
