                        <caesura/>
                         acokṣaṃ duṣṭamutsṛṣṭaṃ pāṣāṇatṛṇaloṣṭavat ||476||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.477">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.477</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dviṣṭaṃ vyuṣitamasvādu pūti cānnaṃ vivarjayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         cirasiddhaṃ sthiraṃ śītamannamuṣṇīkṛtaṃ punaḥ ||477|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.478">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.478</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aśāntam upadagdhaṃ ca tathā svādu na lakṣyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         yadyat svādutaraṃ tattadvidadhyāduttarottaram ||478|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.479">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.479</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prakṣālayed adbhir āsyaṃ bhuñjānasya muhurmuhuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśuddhe rasane tasya rocate 'nnamapūrvavat ||479||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.480">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.480</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svādunā tasya rasanaṃ prathamenātitarpitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         na tathā svādayed anyattasmāt prakṣālyamantarā ||480|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.481">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.481</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saumanasyaṃ balaṃ puṣṭimutsāhaṃ harṣaṇaṃ sukham |
                        <caesura/>
                         svādu sañjanayatyannamasvādu ca viparyayam ||481|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.482">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.482</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhuktvā'pi yat prārthayate bhūyastat svādu bhojanam
                        <caesura/>
                         aśitaścodakaṃ yuktyā bhuñjānaś cāntarā pibet ||482|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.483">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.483</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dantāntaragataṃ cānnaṃ śodhanenāharecchanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryād anirhṛtaṃ taddhi mukhasyāniṣṭagandhatām ||483|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.484">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.484</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jīrṇe 'nne vardhate vāyur vidagdhe pittam eva tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhuktamātre kaphaś cāpi tasmād bhukteritaṃ kapham ||484|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.485">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.485</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhūmenāpohya hṛdyair vā kaṣāyakaṭutiktakaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūgakaṅkolakarpūralavaṅgasumanaḥphalaiḥ ||485||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.486">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.486</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         phalaiḥ kaṭukaṣāyair vā mukhavaiśadyakārakaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tāmbūlapatrasahitaiḥ sugandhair vā vicakṣaṇaḥ ||486|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.487">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.487</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhuktvā rājavadāsīta yāvadannaklamo gataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ pādaśataṃ gatvā vāmapārśvena saṃviśet ||487|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.488">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.488</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śabdānrūpānrasān gandhān sparśāṃś ca manasaḥ priyān |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhuktavānupaseveta tenānnaṃ sādhu tiṣṭhati ||488|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.489">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.489</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śabdarūparasā gandhāḥ sparśāś cāpi jugupsitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         aśucyannaṃ tathā bhuktamatihāsyaṃ ca vāmayet ||489|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.490">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.490</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śayanaṃ cāsanaṃ vā'pi necchedvā'pi dravottaram |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāgnyātapau na plavanaṃ na yānaṃ nāpi vāhanam ||490|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.491">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.491</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na caikarasasevāyāṃ prasajyeta kadācana |
                        <caesura/>
                         śākāvarānnabhūyiṣṭhamamlaṃ ca na samācaret ||491|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.492">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.492</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ekaikaśaḥ samastān vā nādhyaśnīyādrasān sadā
                        <caesura/>
                         prāgbhukte tvavivikte 'gnau dvirannaṃ na samācaret ||492|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.493">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.493</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pūrvabhukte vidagdhe 'nne bhuñjāno hanti pāvakam |
                        <caesura/>
                         mātrāguruṃ pariharedāhāraṃ dravyataś ca yaḥ ||493|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.494">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.494</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         piṣṭānnaṃ naiva bhuñjīta mātrayā vā bubhukṣitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dviguṇaṃ ca pibettoyaṃ sukhaṃ samyak prajīryati
                        <caesura/>
                         peyalehyādyabhakṣyāṇāṃ guru vidyādyathottaram ||494|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.495">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.495</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gurūṇāmardhasauhity aṃ laghūnāṃ tṛptiriṣyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         dravottaro dravaś cāpi na mātrāgururiṣyate ||495|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.496">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.496</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dravāḍhyam api śuṣkaṃ tu samyagevopapadyate
                        <caesura/>
                         viśuṣkamannamabhyastaṃ na pākaṃ sādhu gacchati ||496|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.497">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.497</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         piṇḍīkṛtamasaṅklinnaṃ vidāham upagacchati
                        <caesura/>
                         srotasyannavahe pittaṃ paktau vā yasya tiṣṭhati ||497|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.498">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.498</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vidāhi bhuktamanyadvā tasyāpyannaṃ vidahyate
                        <caesura/>
                         śuṣkaṃ viruddhaṃ viṣṭambhi vahnivyāpadamāvahet ||498|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.499">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.499</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āmaṃ vidagdhaṃ viṣṭabdhaṃ kaphapittānilaistribhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ajīrṇaṃ kecidicchanti caturthaṃ rasaśeṣataḥ ||499|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.500">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.500</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atyambupānādviṣamāśanādvā sandhāraṇāt svapnaviparyayāc ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāle 'pi sātmyaṃ laghu cāpi bhuktamannaṃ na pākaṃ bhajate narasya ||500|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.501">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.501</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         īrṣyābhayakrodhaparikṣatena lubdhena śugdainyanipīḍitena |
                        <caesura/>
                         pradveṣayuktena ca sevyamānamannaṃ na samyak pariṇāmameti ||501|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.502">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.502</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mādhuryamannaṃ gatamāmasañjñaṃ vidagdhasañjñaṃ gatamamlabhāvam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kiñcidvipakvaṃ, bhṛśatodaśūlaṃ viṣṭabdhamānaddhaviruddhavātam ||502|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.503">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.503</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         udgāraśuddhāvapi bhaktakāṅkṣā na jāyate hṛdgurutā ca yasya |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasāvaśeṣeṇa tu saprasekaṃ caturthametat pravadanty ajīrṇam ||503|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.504">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.504</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mūrcchā pralāpo vamathuḥ prasekaḥ sadanaṃ bhramaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         upadravā bhavanty ete maraṇaṃ cāpy ajīrṇataḥ ||504|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.505">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.505</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrāme laṅghanaṃ kāryaṃ, vidagdhe vamanaṃ hitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         viṣṭabdhe svedanaṃ pathyaṃ, rasaśeṣe śayīta ca ||505|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.506">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.506</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vāmayed āśu taṃ tasmād uṣṇena lavaṇāmbunā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāryaṃ vā'naśanaṃ tāvadyāvanna prakṛtiṃ bhajet ||506|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.507">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.507</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         laghukāyamataścainaṃ laṅghanaiḥ samupācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         yāvanna prakṛtisthaḥ syāddoṣataḥ prāṇatas tathā ||507||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.508">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.508</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hitāhitopasaṃyuktamannaṃ samaśanaṃ smṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         bahu stokamakāle vā tajjñeyaṃ viṣamāśanam ||508|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.509">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.509</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ajīrṇe bhujyate yat tu tadadhyaśanamucyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         trayametannihanty āśu bahūnvyādhīnkaroti vā ||509|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.510">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.510</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         annaṃ vidagdhaṃ hi narasya śīghraṃ śītāmbunā vai paripākameti |
                        <caesura/>
                         taddhyasya śaity ena nihanti pittamākledibhāvācca nayatyadhastāt ||510|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.511">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.511</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vidahyate yasya tu bhuktamātre dahyeta hṛtkoṣṭhagalaṃ ca yasya |
                        <caesura/>
                         drākṣābhayāṃ mākṣikasamprayuktāṃ līḍhvā'bhayāṃ vā sa sukhaṃ labheta ||511|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.512">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.512</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhaved ajīrṇaṃ prati yasya śaṅkā snigdhasya jantorbalino 'nnakāle |
                        <caesura/>
                         prātaḥ saśuṇṭhīmabhayāmaśaṅko bhuñjīta samprāśya hitaṃ hitārthī ||512|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.513">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.513</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svalpaṃ yadā doṣavibaddhamāmaṃ līnaṃ na tejaḥpathamāvṛṇoti | bhavatyajīrṇe
                        'pi tadā bubhukṣā yā mandabuddhiṃ viṣavannihanti ||513|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.514">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.514</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata urdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi guṇānāṃ karmavistaram |
                        <caesura/>
                         karmabhis tv anumīyante nānādravyāśrayā guṇāḥ ||514|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.515">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.515</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hlādanaḥ stambhanaḥ śīto mūrcchātṛṭsvedadāhajit |
                        <caesura/>
                         uṣṇastadviparītaḥ syātpācanaś ca viśeṣataḥ ||515|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.516">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.516</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snehamārdavakṛt snigdho balavarṇakaras tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         rūkṣastadviparītaḥ syādviśeṣāt stambhanaḥ kharaḥ ||516|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.517">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.517</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         picchilo jīvano balyaḥ sandhānaḥ śleṣmalo guruḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśado viparīto 'smāt kledācūṣaṇaropaṇaḥ ||517|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.518">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.518</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dāhapākakarastīkṣṇaḥ srāvaṇo, mṛduranyathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sādopalepabalakṛdgurustarpaṇabṛṃhaṇaḥ ||518|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.519">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.519</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         laghustadviparītaḥ syāl lekhano ropaṇas tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         daśādyāḥ karmataḥ proktās teṣāṃ karmaviśeṣaṇaiḥ ||519|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.520">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.520</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         daśaivānyān pravakṣyāmi dravādīṃstānnibodha me |
                        <caesura/>
                         dravaḥ prakledanaḥ, sāndraḥ sthūlaḥ syādbandhakārakaḥ ||520|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.521">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.521</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ślakṣṇaḥ picchilavajjñeyaḥ karkaśo viśado yathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhānubandhī sūkṣmaś ca sugandho rocano mṛduḥ ||521|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.522">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.522</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         durgandho viparīto 'smāddhṛllāsārucikārakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saro 'nulomanaḥ prokto, mando yātrākaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||522|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.523">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.523</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vyavāyī cākhilaṃ dehaṃ vyāpya pākāya kalpate |
                        <caesura/>
                         vikāsī vikasannevaṃ dhātubandhān vimokṣayet ||523|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.524">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.524</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āśukārī tathā''śutvād dhāvatyambhasi tailavat |
                        <caesura/>
                         sūkṣmas tu saukṣmyāt sūkṣmeṣu srotaḥsvanusaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||524|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.525">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.525</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         guṇā viṃśatirity evaṃ yathāvatparikīrtitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sampravakṣyāmyataścordhvamāhāragatiniścayam ||525|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.526">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.526</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcabhūtātmake dehe hyāhāraḥ pāñcabhautikaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vipakvaḥ pañcadhā samyagguṇān svānabhivardhayet ||526|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.527">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.527</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         avidagdhaḥ kaphaṃ, pittaṃ vidagdhaḥ, pavanaṃ punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyagvipakvo niḥsāra āhāraḥ paribṛṃhayet ||527|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.528">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.528</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viṇmūtramāhāramalaḥ sāraḥ prāgīrito rasaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa tu vyānena vikṣiptaḥ sarvān dhātūn pratarpayet ||528|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.529">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.529</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphaḥ pittaṃ malaḥ kheṣu svedaḥ syānnakharoma ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         netraviṭ tvakṣu ca sneho dhātūnāṃ kramaśo malāḥ ||529|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.530">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.530</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         divā vibuddhe hṛdaye jāgrataḥ puṇḍarīkavat |
                        <caesura/>
                         annamaklinnadhātutvād ajīrṇe 'pi hitaṃ niśi ||530|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.531">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.531</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛdi sammīlite rātrau prasuptasya viśeṣataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         klinnavisrastadhātutvād ajīrṇe na hitaṃ divā ||531|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.532">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.532</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         imaṃ vidhiṃ yo 'numataṃ mahāmunernṛparṣimukhyasya paṭheddhi yatnataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa bhūmipālāya vidhātumauṣadhaṃ mahātmanāṃ cārhati sūrisattamaḥ ||532|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.trailer">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 1.46.trailer</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         iti bhagavatā śrīdhanvantariṇopadiṣṭāyāṃ tacchiṣyeṇa maharṣiṇā suśrutena
                        viracitāyāṃ suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne ṣaṭcatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||46||
